# Republic of the Philippines Department of Health OFFICE OF THE SECRETARY

#### **AUTHORIZATION**

In accordance with the authority vested on the Secretary of Health, it is hereby declared that the policies and standards in the Procedures Manual for Government Hospitals, Third Edition shall guide the organization, management, operations and activities of the various services, departments, sections, and unit in the Department of Health (DOH) hospitals. The Manual may be used as reference by the local government and other hospitals and health facilities.

This Authorization shall take effect upon signing, and shall remain in effect until revised and updated by the DOH.

FRANCISCO T. DI QUE III, MD, MSc Secretary of Health

![](_page_4_Picture_0.jpeg)

# Republic of the Philippines Department of Health OFFICE OF THE SECRETARY

#### MESSAGE FROM THE SECRETARY OF HEALTH

![](_page_4_Picture_3.jpeg)

Through the enactment of the Universal Health Care (UHC) by virtue of Republic Act No. 11223, the Department of Health (DOH) continues to lead the nation's development of a productive, resilient, equitable, and people-centered health system, with the central goal of ensuring that all Filipinos gain equitable access to quality and affordable health care goods and services, while also guaranteeing their protection against financial risk.

The DOH realises the fact that the demand for health services shall continue to grow, and thus recognizes that the only appropriate response to this is the continuous improvement of the operations of hospitals and other health facilities, as well as

the continuous development of the standards and policies relevant to health facility development. It is on this significant premise that this manual is crafted.

This Procedures Manual for Government Hospitals resonates from the strategies outlined in the F1 Plus' Service Delivery Pillar. The standards defined in this manual shall serve as guide and reference for hospital administrators, health service providers, and hospital support staff as they uphold the mandates of the UHC Act with improved computer-based information systems.

We are confident that these standards shall set our health facilities upon the right direction to ensure their readiness for the future of Philippine public health. This manual has also been imbued with the learnings gained by the entirety of the health sector from the global pandemic response. Through our steadfast work and enthusiastic collaboration to steer the entire Philippine health sector, we are optimistic that the vision of Universal Health Care for all Filipinos shall be ultimately achieved.

FRANCISCO T. DI QUE III, MD, MSc

Secretary of Health

![](_page_5_Picture_0.jpeg)

### Republic of the Philippines Department of Health

#### OFFICE OF THE SECRETARY

#### **MESSAGE**

![](_page_5_Picture_4.jpeg)

The Department of Health's vision is for Filipinos to be among the healthiest in Southeast Asia and in Asia. The Universal Health Care (UHC) and the DOH's FOURmula One Plus for Health of F1 Plus provided a strategic direction in realizing this vision. The Health Facilities and Infrastructure Development Team (HFIDT) seeks to ensure the availability of adequate health services, foster proficient management of health sector resources for health facility development, and ensure the efficient and effective health facility

operations with the use of technology to empower patients through a people-centered approach to health services.

We proactively support the DOH's objective of providing all Filipinos better access to appropriate health care services without experiencing financial hardship. We serve with values of professionalism, integrity, responsiveness, compassion and excellence, to produce a more responsive health system that could guarantee better health outcomes for patients across all levels of care.

The Health Facility Development Bureau (HFDB), one of the Bureaus under the HFIDT, has undertaken the development of the **Procedures Manual for Government Hospitals**, in accordance with their mandate to develop policies, standards and plans related to health facilities and hospitals. This manual shall serve as the health facilities' reference in implementing the standard operating procedures of the different units or services of the hospital to ensure continuous quality improvement in the delivery of health care services.

We invite hospital administrators, medical and allied medical personnel and support staff, all other stakeholders, as well as other hospitals under the administration of the local government units, to promote and adopt these standards, to guide the determination to elevate the quality of our country's health care system.

Thank you and more power to all!

LILIBETH C. DAVID, MD, MPH, MPM, CESO I

Undersecretary of Health

Health Facilities and Infrastructure Development Team

![](_page_6_Picture_0.jpeg)

#### Republic of the Philippines Department of Health

#### OFFICE OF THE SECRETARY

#### **FOREWORD**

The Health Facility Development Bureau (HFDB) of the Department of Health (DOH) is at the forefront in implementing the Integrated Hospital Operations and Management Program (IHOMP), which aims to standardize the management systems and procedures to enhance the preventive, promotive and curative roles of government and private hospitals.

Cognizant of the ever-changing milieu and the variance of procedures and services across the different hospitals, the HFDB constantly renews and consolidates the standards and operation systems of hospitals nationwide. Through development workshops and consultative meetings with key technical advisers, the HFDB ensures that information contained in this updated edition of the **Procedures Manual for Government Hospitals** are evidence-based and relevant.

The updated guidelines have been anchored to the fundamental premises of Universal Health Care (UHC) and the DOH's main strategic platform to boost UHC, the *FOUR*mula One Plus for Health (F1+). It has incorporated the patient's vantage point and has considered how it integrates with the hospital administration. Moreover, this manual provides guidance on the implementation of information systems such as the DOH Integrated Hospital Operations Management Information System (iHOMIS) in response to permeating technological advancements.

This Manual will be periodically reviewed and revised to address new ideas that may arise overtime and shall be updated as new applicable regulations and guidelines are published. The HFDB encourages feedback from various stakeholders and users of this manual. But meanwhile, I hope that this manual will serve a useful purpose, especially for hospital administrators who handle a broad array of constituents and concerns.

MA. THERESA G. VERA, MD, MSc, MHA, CESO III

Director IV

Health Facility Development Bureau

### **ACKNOWLEDGEMENT**

We would like to extend our sincerest appreciation to the different members of various expert groups of the different hospital services. The development of the **Procedures Manual for Government Hospitals** would have not been completed without the efforts and participation of these select technical working group members from the Emergency Department, Pharmacy, Medical Social Work, Nutrition-Dietetics, Laboratory, Nursing Service, Patient Safety, Infection Prevention and Control, etc. Their expert inputs and knowledge has added value and dignified the very essence of this material.

Also, this initiative has been accomplished through the tireless commitment and dedication from the advisers and technical staff of the Health Facility Development Bureau. We are grateful for the hard work that you have put into the creation of this manual. Their cooperation in the development of this manual is a manifestation of the HFDB's core values of excellence, integrity, collaborativeness, people-centeredness and team Work, which they have all proudly exemplified.

We would also like to extend our gratitude to the different offices in the Department of Health, namely the Procurement Service, the Knowledge Management and Information Technology Service, especially the IHOMIS Team, and the Administrative Service. Their generosity in sharing your expertise has helped in ensuring the refinement of the contents of this manual.

Last but definitely not the least, we would like to thank the DOH Hospitals who have provided their inputs and concurred in the consolidated procedures in this manual. Their enthusiastic contribution to the manual development has proven their commitment to continuous quality improvement in the provision of facility-based health care to Filipinos. With their full support, and as we enjoin our other stakeholders' cooperation, we could effectively steer the health sector towards the achievement of universal health care.

### **DEFINITION OF TERMS**

| Terminology                                  | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
|----------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Annual Operational Planning                  | The version of the Local Investment Plan for Health (LIPH)<br>that is prepared every year of the three-year planning cycle.<br>this is an LGU spending plan document that sets the budgetary<br>resources it expects to have for the year and the performance<br>targets for this period. It may also refer to the indicative<br>operational plan or OPlan for the succeeding fiscal year of the<br>DOH. It is the basis of the budget proposal of the DOH Units<br>or programs as opposed to the work and financial plan (WFP),<br>which is based in the NEP or the GAA. |
| Annual<br>Procurement<br>Plan<br>(APP)       | An itemized list of goods and services, infrastructure projects<br>and consulting services required for a calendar year planned<br>for procurement out of the funds allotted to an agency.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Authorized Borrower                          | A person authorized by the owner of the health record or by a<br>legitimate borrower to gain access to the specific record in<br>accordance with the law and hospital policy/order.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Bidding Documents                            | Documents issued by the Procuring Entity as the bases for<br>bids, furnishing all information necessary for a prospective<br>bidder to prepare a bid for the infrastructure projects, goods,<br>and/or consulting services required by the Procuring Entity.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Bromage Score                                | The most frequently used measure of motor block. In this<br>scale, the intensity of motor block is assessed by the patient's<br>ability to move their lower extremities.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Chief of the Administrative<br>Service (CAS) | An officer occupying the highest position in the Hospital<br>Operations and Patient Support Service, formerly known as<br>the Administrative Service, such as Chief Administrative<br>Officer (CAO) or Supervising Administrative Officer (SAO).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Condemnation                                 | The act of destroying by burning, pounding, throwing, or any<br>other method by which the valueless property of the<br>government is disposed beyond economic recovery.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Cost Centers                                 | Departments/sections/units of the hospital which does not<br>generate income from its operations.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |

| Disposal                                                                                 | The act of parting with, alienation of, or giving up supplies or<br>property. It is the end of the life cycle of a government<br>property.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Donation                                                                                 | Assets/properties acquired through contribution or donations<br>from the private sector, other government agencies both local<br>and foreign and non-government organization.                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Health Facility                                                                          | An institution that has health care as its core service, function<br>or business. Health care pertains to the maintenance or<br>improvement of the health of individuals or populations<br>through the prevention, diagnosis, treatment, rehabilitation<br>and chronic management of disease, illness, injury, and other<br>physical and mental ailments or impairments of human<br>beings. |
| Inspection                                                                               | Examination of supplies or services (including<br>materials and<br>components) to determine whether the supplies and services<br>conform to contract requirement.                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Insurers                                                                                 | Refer to local health insurance officers of PhilHealth, health<br>maintenance organizations and private health insurance<br>companies issued certificates of authority by the Insurance<br>Commission, and those identified by DOH and PhilHealth.                                                                                                                                          |
| Integrated<br>Hospital<br>Operations and Management<br>Information<br>System<br>(IHOMIS) | A computer-based information system developed by the<br>Department<br>of<br>Health<br>-<br>Knowledge<br>Management<br>and<br>Information Technology Service (DOH-KMITS)                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Integrated<br>Hospital<br>Operations and Management<br>Program (IHOMP)                   | Refers to the program under the Health Facility Development<br>Bureau (HFDB) that ensures the implementation of standards<br>and guidelines<br>aimed to improve efficiency and effectiveness<br>of health care services through creation and use of information<br>for clinical, administrative, and monitoring purposes in<br>hospitals and other health facilities.                       |
| Inventory                                                                                | An itemized list of supplies or property on hand containing<br>designation or description of each specific article with its<br>valuation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |

| Negotiated Procurement                   | A method of procurement of goods, infrastructure projects and<br>consulting services, whereby the procuring entity directly<br>negotiates<br>a<br>contract<br>with<br>a<br>technically,<br>legally,<br>and<br>financially capable supplier, contractor, consultant or, where<br>allowed, an individual consultant, only in cases provided<br>under Sec. 53 of Republic Act No. 9184 and Sec 53, Rule XVI<br>of its Implementing Rules and Regulations.           |
|------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Nutrition<br>and<br>Dietetics<br>Service | It is one of the major services of the hospital and plays an<br>integral part of the total patient care service. This is organized<br>and integrated with other units and departments/services of a<br>hospital and is designed to ensure the provision of optimal<br>nutrition care and quality food service.                                                                                                                                                   |
| Nutrition Care Process (NCP)             | Systematic<br>problem-solving<br>method<br>that<br>nutrition<br>and<br>dietetics professionals utilize to critically think and make<br>decisions to address nutrition-related problems and provide<br>safe and effective quality nutrition care. NCP consists of four<br>distinct steps which are interrelated and interconnected:<br>Nutrition<br>Assessment,<br>Nutrition<br>Diagnosis,<br>Nutrition<br>Intervention, and Nutrition Monitoring and Evaluation. |
| Partograph                               | Partograph is a<br>Greek word meaning<br>"Labor Curve".<br>Partograph comes as a pre-printed one-page form on which<br>labor<br>observations<br>are<br>recorded, it<br>provides<br>a graphic<br>overview of the progress of labor and records information<br>about maternal and fetal condition during labor.                                                                                                                                                    |
| Patient Health Record/Health<br>Record   | Formerly known as Medical Record, is a chronological<br>written account of a patient's examination and treatment that<br>includes the patient's medical history and complaints, the<br>physician's physical findings, the results of diagnostic tests<br>and procedures, and medications and therapeutic procedures.                                                                                                                                             |
| Point of Service<br>(POS)                | Refers to the program provided by the General Appropriations<br>Act (GAA) 2017 to register non-PhilHealth members into the<br>National Health Insurance Program (NHIP) thereby providing<br>them immediate entitlement to PhilHealth benefits.                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Preventive Maintenance                   | Correct operation and servicing, systematic inspection and<br>detection and correction of the cause of equipment failures<br>before they occur or develop into major defects.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |

| Project<br>Procurement<br>Management Plan (PPMP) | It is an itemized list of the estimated quantity of supplies or<br>property needed for the entire fiscal year by the end-user unit,<br>with complete description as to kind, quantity, quality and the<br>estimated cost |
|--------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Property Accountability                          | The obligation imposed by lawful order or regulation of an<br>official for keeping accurate record of property. The person<br>having this obligation may or may not have actual possession<br>of the property.           |
| Revenue Centers                                  | Departments/sections/units of the hospital which generate<br>income from its operations.                                                                                                                                 |
| Software Maintenance                             | Activities intended to keep the IHOMIS useful at all times.                                                                                                                                                              |
| Unit-Dose Drug Distribution<br>System (UDDDS)    | A<br>pharmacy-coordinated<br>method<br>of<br>dispensing<br>and<br>controlling medication in organized healthcare settings.                                                                                               |

xiv

# **PART I INTRODUCTION**

#### **BACKGROUND AND RATIONALE**

The approval of Republic Act No. 11223, also known as the Universal Health Care (UHC) Act is a major milestone in the healthcare system of the Philippines. The Act aims to ensure that all Filipinos are guaranteed with equitable access to quality and affordable health care goods and services, and protected against financial risk.<sup>1</sup> One of the strategic thrust to attain this is through Improved Access to Quality Hospitals and Health Care Facilities. In line with the thrust of the Department of Health (DOH), the Health Facility Development Bureau (HFDB) is tasked to lead in the development of health facility standards, policies, programs and plans including structural and clinical management of the different services, departments and units.<sup>2</sup> These standards aim to provide a people-centered approach for the delivery of health services, and to ensure accessibility of essential quality health services at appropriate levels of care.

To achieve universal health coverage for all Filipinos, the expansion of the health services is inevitable. Thus, the need for a more comprehensive and clear set of procedures geared towards better performance in the health system. The hospitals and other health facilities have been continuously improving, not only in terms of their infrastructure and equipment, but also in terms of the quality of services they render.

As a guide to the implementation and management of these health services especially in government hospitals, HFDB is currently updating the manual of standards for each services and departments under the Integrated Hospital Operations and Management Program (IHOMP). This procedures manual is best used in conjunction with the following manuals:

- 1. Manual of Organization and Management of the Administrative and Finance Service for Hospitals;
- 2. Hospital Property and Supply Management Manual;
- 3. Hospital Nursing Service Administration Manual;
- 4. Hospital Pharmacy Management Manual;
- 5. Hospital Nutrition and Dietetics Service Management Manual;
- 6. Manual for Medical Social Workers Fifth Edition;
- 7. Manual of Standards for Infection Control in Health Care Facilities;
- 8. Quality Management Systems in Clinical Laboratories;
- 9. Manual of Standards and Guidelines on the Management of Hospital Emergency Department; and
- 10. Health Care Waste Management Manual
- 11. Revised Organizational Structure and Staffing Standards for Government Hospitals

The development of health facility standards, policies and plans; likewise, extends to the development of information and communication technology (ICT) infrastructure. In modern times, the health system also strives to be at par with the advancement of technology, specifically those that are beneficial to the various health facilities. For hospitals, the integrated Hospital Operations and Management Information System (iHOMIS) was developed through the Knowledge Management and Information Technology Service (KMITS).

<sup>1</sup> Sec. 3 (b) Republic Act No. 11223, 23 July 2018

<sup>2</sup> DOH Department Memorandum No. 2019-0010, Functional Directions for the Health Facilities and Infrastructure Development Team

 The system was designed based on the manual of standards and operations of the hospitals under IHOMP as enumerated above. It was initially implemented in selected DOH, LGU and private hospitals in 2003. Throughout the years, the functionalities of iHOMIS expanded into generating needed data for various disease registries and other information systems. Currently, iHOMIS has integrated the requirements of the Philippine Health Insurance Corporation (PhilHealth) to enable the submission of needed data for membership verification and claims processing. Moreover, in coordination with the Commission on Audit (COA), the system is envisioned to link the financial aspect of the system to the electronic New Government Accounting System (eNGAS).

The DOH through its platform *FOUR*mula One (F1 Plus) for Health recognizes the relevance of generating and utilizing data and information for evidence-based planning, policy development, program implementation and decision making in the health sector.<sup>3</sup> Thus, all health facilities shall be required to submit health-related and financial data and to make accessible to the public prices of health services and goods being offered. Given this intent, all health service providers and insurers shall maintain a health information system that is consistent with DOH standards.<sup>4</sup>

In response to this directive, a workshop for the development of a *Procedures Manual for Government Hospitals* was conducted in January 28-31, 2020. The manual is an output from the expertise of selected Technical Working Group (TWG) members of the different manuals being reviewed and updated, technical staff of HFDB and DOH-retained hospitals. Likewise, the members of the iHOMIS Team participated in the said workshop to provide a perspective on the technicalities of the system.

The manual seeks to provide guidance and assistance in the complete translation of the standards into the iHOMIS. In addition to this, the manual seeks to ensure the compliance of the hospitals to the standards even after its translation into the hospital information system.

#### **OBJECTIVES**

The manual seeks to provide guidance in the incorporation, translation, and upgrading of the manual standards into the iHOMIS. Moreover, the manual aims to provide government hospitals with updated and integrated procedures that shall assist them in the delivery of quality health services for all Filipinos.

#### **SCOPE AND COVERAGE**

The manual consists of general procedures under the different services and departments available in a hospital. These procedures have been written in such a way as to accommodate and provide discretion to the hospitals in terms of the specific details and strategy in its implementation, while still being consistent with the standards.

<sup>3</sup> DOH Administrative Order No. 2018-0014, Strategic Framework and Implementing Guidelines for *FOUR*mula One Plus for Health

<sup>4</sup> Sec. 36, Republic Act No. 11223, 23 July 2018

The manual is applicable to government hospitals; however, the following limitations have been identified:

- 1. Provides only minimum required steps in a procedure, which gives the hospitals prerogative to introduce modifications *(i.e additional steps/procedures, or variation in forms, etc)*. Provided, that a.) DOH standards are still complied with, especially in the computerization or automation of hospital systems; and b.) major steps are still present to ensure the same desired outcome/output.
- 2. The procedures aim to provide the systems administrators/computer programmers an overview of simplified standards to assist them in the translation or upgrading of the system.
- 3. The procedures shall be understood and interpreted in consonance with the manual of standards, policies and plans of the hospitals.

# **PART II DESCRIPTION AND FLOW CHARTS OF THE PROCEDURES**

#### **DESCRIPTION and FLOW CHARTS of the PROCEDURES**

This part includes the description and corresponding flowchart of the procedures of the different services and departments in a hospital.

A hospital is defined as a place devoted primarily to the maintenance and operation of health facilities for the diagnosis, treatment and care of individuals suffering from illness, disease, injury or deformity, or in need of obstetrical or other surgical, medical and nursing care. <sup>5</sup> Hospitals are classified based on ownership as government and private. A government health facility may be under the national government, DOH, Local Government Unit (LGU), Department of National Defense (DND), Philippine National Police (PNP), Department of Justice (DOJ), State Universities and Colleges (SUCs), Government Owned and Controlled Corporations (GOCC) and others. Moreover, they are classified according to their functional capacity as Level 1, Level 2 and Level 3 (Teaching/Training).

Table 1 shows the summary of the procedures included in this manual. These procedures are best construed when used together with the manual of standards under IHOMP.

|                                        | Name of Service/Department/Area                            | No. of Procedures |  |

<sup>5</sup> Department of Health (DOH) Administrative Order no. 2012-0012, Rules and Regulations Governing the New Classification Hospitals and Other Health Facilities in the Philippines, Definition of Terms and Acronyms, July 2012

### **Chapter 1 Medical and Nursing Service Procedures**

The Medical Services consists of various departments, sections and units that form part and contribute to the overall efficiency of hospital operations. Likewise, the Nursing service is a vital component in the hospital that provides direct and indirect patient care. These services constitute the largest number of the medical and healthcare professionals and is the most predominant components of the hospitals.

| 7.<br>Informs the physician on duty of new<br>admission<br>and<br>refer<br>pertinent<br>findings necessary for the plan of<br>care or management.                                                         | Nurse     |                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 8.<br>Documents patient care activities,<br>observations, interventions through<br>Focus, Data, Actions, Result (FDAR)<br>and<br>medications<br>and<br>treatment<br>given/administered.                   | Nurse     | Patient's Health<br>Record; Nurses<br>Notes;<br>Medication sheet;<br>IV Fluid Sheet;<br>Intake and Output<br>Monitoring sheet;<br>Temperature,<br>Pulse, Respiratory<br>rate (TPR); Vital<br>signs |
| 9.<br>Completes Admission documents in<br>the Chart (ie History, PE and 1st<br>Ward notes).                                                                                                               | Physician | Patient's Health<br>Record                                                                                                                                                                         |
| 10.<br>Update the chart for any progress or<br>new orders<br><br>Facilitate<br>referral<br>to<br>other<br>services/ specialty (if applicable)                                                            | Physician | Patient's Health<br>Record<br>Doctor's Notes                                                                                                                                                       |
| 11.<br>Request Nurse on Duty to read back<br>new orders if there are any.                                                                                                                                 | Physician | Doctor's Notes                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 12.<br>Facilitates new orders (if applicable,<br>documents<br>patient<br>care<br>activities,<br>observations, interventions through<br>FDAR<br>and<br>medications<br>and<br>treatment given/administered. | Nurse     | Patient's Health<br>Record; Nurses<br>Notes;<br>Medication sheet;<br>IV Fluid Sheet;<br>Intake and Output<br>Monitoring sheet;<br>Temperature,<br>Pulse, Respiratory<br>rate (TPR); Vital<br>signs |

#### **F. General Discharge Procedure**

#### **9. General Discharge Procedure**

| Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Person/Department<br>Responsible                                        | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                       |
|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Gives<br>order<br>for<br>discharge<br>and<br>instructions.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Physician                                                               | Emergency<br>assessment and<br>disposition form;<br>Doctor's order sheet;<br>clinical cover sheet |
| 2.<br>Carries<br>out<br>doctor's<br>order<br>and<br>provides<br>discharge<br>planning/aftercare<br>instructions<br>to<br>patient and caregiver which may<br>include but is not limited to the<br>following:<br>a.<br>Medications;<br>b.<br>Follow-up;<br>c.<br>Warning signs;<br>d.<br>Post-partum care; and<br>e.<br>Dietary Instructions. | Nurse<br>and other<br>allied health<br>service/department<br>concerned. | Discharge summary;<br>WHO Safe Child<br>Checklist                                                 |
| 3.<br>Consolidates<br>all<br>charges<br>and<br>forwards to billing section.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Clerk                                                                   |                                                                                                   |
| 4.<br>Informs<br>all<br>revenue<br>centers<br>and<br>MSWD that patient is for discharge.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Billing and Claims<br>Department (BCD)                                  |                                                                                                   |
| 5.<br>Revenue centers forwards remaining<br>charge slips to Billing and Claims<br>Department.<br>MSWD<br>forwards<br>classification and funding grants to<br>Billing and Claims Department.                                                                                                                                                 | Revenue centers and<br>MSWD                                             |                                                                                                   |
| 6.<br>Generates<br>Statement<br>of<br>Account<br>(SOA).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | BCD                                                                     | Statement of<br>Account (SOA)                                                                     |
| 7.<br>Provides<br>copy<br>of<br>the<br>SOA<br>and<br>explains to patient/caregiver.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | BCD                                                                     |                                                                                                   |
| 8.<br>Refers patient/caregiver to the Cash<br>Operations Department (COD) for<br>payment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | BCD                                                                     | Official Receipt                                                                                  |
| 9.<br>Processes<br>payment<br>and<br>issues<br>discharge<br>clearance<br>to<br>patient/caregiver.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Cash Operations<br>Department (COD)                                     | Discharge Clearance<br>and Official Receipt.                                                      |
| 10.<br>Receives<br>accomplished<br>discharge<br>clearance from patient/caregiver.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Staff                                                                   | Clearance/discharge<br>slip                                                                       |
| 11.<br>Accomplishes<br>discharge<br>summary<br>and completes entry in chart.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Physician                                                               | Discharge summary,<br>Patient Health<br>Record                                                    |
| 12.<br>Issues discharge summary, clearance<br>and gate pass to patient/caregiver.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Nurse                                                                   | Discharge summary,<br>Clearance.                                                                  |

#### **G. Procedure for Disposition of Cadaver**

#### **10. Disposal of Cadaver**

| Description                                                | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document |
|------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------|
| 1.<br>Receives endorsed Cadaver with                       | Morgue Technician                | Cadaver' Tag,               |
| accomplished identification.                               |                                  | Cadaver ID<br>form          |
| 2.<br>Registers in the Morgue Registry                     | Morgue Technician                | Morgue Registry             |
| Logbook                                                    |                                  | Logbook                     |
| 3.<br>Verifies<br>endorsement<br>note<br>and               | Morgue Technician                | Morgue Registry             |
| cadaver tag to determine if cadaver                        |                                  | Logbook;                    |
| is infectious.                                             |                                  | Nurse's                     |
| <br>For<br>Non-Infectious,                                |                                  | Endorsement                 |
| Cadaver are deposited in the                               |                                  | Form                        |
| Morgue Freezer                                             |                                  |                             |
| <br>For<br>Infectious<br>Cadaver,                         |                                  |                             |
| must ensure that it is placed                              |                                  |                             |
| in an air-tight cadaver bag                                |                                  |                             |
| prior to deposit in morgue                                 |                                  |                             |
| freezer                                                    |                                  |                             |
| 4.<br>If Cadaver is unclaimed (Retention                   | Morgue Technician                | Hospital Standard           |
| Time is 3-5 days as stated in the                          |                                  | Operating                   |
| Sanitation Code of the Philippines):                       |                                  | Procedures (SOP)            |
| Follows<br>the<br>procedure/guidelines                     |                                  |                             |
| for disposal of unclaimed cadaver                          |                                  |                             |
| and submits/refers list of unclaimed                       |                                  |                             |
| to the MSWD                                                |                                  |                             |
| If cadaver is claimed:                                     |                                  |                             |
|                                                           |                                  |                             |
| Receive Notice of Release<br>of Cadaver                    |                                  |                             |
| <br>Verify identity of claimant                           |                                  |                             |
|                                                            |                                  |                             |
| <br>Identification of cadaver by<br>the verified claimant |                                  |                             |
|                                                            |                                  |                             |
| <br>Verify that proper vehicle<br>for transport is used   |                                  |                             |
| 5.<br>Records the release of Cadaver in                    | Morgue Technician                | Morgue Registry             |
| the Morgue Registry Logbook                                |                                  | Logbook                     |
|                                                            |                                  |                             |

|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1. Orders transfer of patient post-<br>partum.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Resident on Duty / OB            | Patient Health<br>Record                                        |
| <ol> <li>Checks status of mother and baby and coordinates with Admitting section.</li> <li>If the status of the mother and baby is critical, refer to PACU/NICU.</li> <li>If not critical, then refer to OB ward/room.</li> <li>Refer to chart no. XX for OB ward admission process.</li> </ol> | Delivery Room (DR)<br>Nurse      | Patient Health<br>Record                                        |
| 3. Completes the Delivery Room (DR) charting using the Focus-Data-Actions-Response (FDAR) method and accomplishes Certificate of Live Birth (COLB)                                                                                                                                              | DR Nurse                         | DR Charting<br>(FDAR); COLB                                     |
| 4. Accomplishes charge slip and forwards to Billing Section                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | DR Nurse                         | Charge slip                                                     |
| 5. Endorses Mother and Baby to: 5.1 PACU/NICU for critical care; or 5.2 OB ward/room for non-critical care                                                                                                                                                                                      | DR Nurse                         | Checklist<br>Medication<br>Medical Record<br>Latest Vital Signs |

| 1.<br>Explains the procedure to the patient<br>and family.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Surgeon                          | Physician's<br>Admitting Order<br>Sheet<br>Informed consent<br>form (Surgery) |
| 2.<br>Facilitate<br>signing<br>of<br>informed<br>consent.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Surgeon / Ward Nurse             | Informed Consent<br>Form                                                      |
| Note:<br>Check policy on validity of informed<br>consent.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                                  |                                                                               |
| 3.<br>Writes the order for surgery and<br>schedule,<br>including<br>referral<br>to<br>anesthesia, internal medicine for co<br>management,<br>prophylactic<br>antibiotic,<br>intravenous<br>hydration,<br>schedule<br>of<br>fasting,<br>bowel<br>preparation<br>if needed.                                                                           | Surgeon                          | Patient Database<br>Form;<br>Histopathology<br>Request Form                   |
| 4.<br>Endorses the orders to the nurse-on<br>duty.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Surgeon                          | Patient Database<br>Form;<br>Histopathology<br>Request Form                   |
| 5.<br>Accomplishes<br>the<br>following:<br>Patient<br>Database<br>Form,<br>Safe<br>Surgery Checklist, Histopathology<br>Request Form.                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Surgeon                          | Patient Database<br>Form;<br>Histopathology<br>Request Form                   |
| 6.<br>Places Surgical Marking (if needed)<br>to ensure correct site.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Surgeon                          | Patient Database<br>Form;<br>Histopathology<br>Request Form                   |
| 7.<br>Carries-out doctor's order after read<br>back.<br>7.1<br>Refer<br>to<br>MSWD<br>for<br>Psychosocial interventions.<br>7.2<br>If Cardio-Pulmonary Clearance<br>is<br>needed,<br>refers<br>to<br>Internal<br>Medicine<br>(IM)<br>or<br>other<br>appropriate<br>department.<br>If<br>cleared, or no CP Clearance<br>needed, Proceed to number 4. | Ward Nurse                       | Patient's chart                                                               |

| 7.3<br>If not cleared, facilitates<br>orders<br>by other departments needed for<br>clearance then refer back<br>to<br>appropriate department.                       |                  |                     |
|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------|---------------------|
| 8.<br>Prepares OR proposal form.                                                                                                                                    | Ward Nurse       | OR Proposal<br>Form |
| 9.<br>Forwards OR Proposal to OR.                                                                                                                                   | Ward Nurse       |                     |
| 10.<br>Receipt of OR Proposal and makes<br>necessary preparation for operation                                                                                      | OR Nurse         |                     |
| 11.<br>Schedules proposal for operation<br>and informs Anesthesia Department<br>of OR Proposal.                                                                     | OR Nurse         |                     |
| 12.<br>Visits and assesses the patient and<br>make pre-operative order (i.e. NPO;<br>IVF medications, etc.) Also assesses<br>the need for further<br>labs, specific | Anesthesiologist |                     |
| clearances,<br>makes<br>recommendations for optimization<br>of patient for surgery.                                                                                 | Internist        |                     |
| 13.<br>Informs<br>surgeon<br>of<br>anesthesia<br>department's orders and carries<br>out<br>order of the Anesthesiologist.                                           | Ward Nurse       |                     |
| 14.<br>Requests<br>for<br>Pre-operative<br>medications and other medications<br>needed intraoperatively.                                                            | Ward Nurse       |                     |

|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Receives the patient from the ward<br>nurse to the OR complex.<br>1.1<br>Confirms<br>patient's<br>identity,                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Circulating Nurse                                           | Patient ID Wrist<br>Tag      |
| surgical site, consent, etc.<br>1.2<br>Checks<br>if<br>all<br>pre-operative<br>medications were given and all<br>materials for the procedure are<br>available for use. Informs the<br>anesthesiologist of the patient.                                                                                                                                                                              |                                                             | Pre-Operative<br>Checklist   |
| 2.<br>Validates Pre-operative checklist and<br>reassessment of the patient done<br>2.1<br>Anesthesiologists may opt to give                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Circulating Nurses                                          | Pre-Operative<br>Checklist   |
| pre-medications (i.e. sedatives)<br>to the patient, then give oxygen<br>here.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Anesthesiologist                                            |                              |
| 3.<br>Transfers the patient to the operating<br>room and on to the operating table                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Anesthesiologist<br>Circulating nurse/<br>Nursing attendant |                              |
| 4.<br>Accomplishes the SIGN-IN part of<br>Surgical<br>Safety<br>Checklist.<br>The<br>following has been confirmed:<br>a.<br>Identity<br>b.<br>Site<br>c.<br>Procedure<br>d.<br>Consent<br>e.<br>Site Marking                                                                                                                                                                                        | Circulating<br>Nurse/Anesthesiologist                       | Surgical Safety<br>Checklist |
| 5.<br>Prepares the following:<br>5.1 Takes<br>and records<br>the initial vital<br>signs of the patient.<br>5.2 Checks materials needed<br>for the<br>induction<br>of<br>anesthesia<br>are<br>readily available.<br>5.2.1 Checks<br>the patency of the<br>intravenous<br>fluid<br>line<br>anesthesia<br>machine,<br>any<br>emergency<br>medications,<br>checks<br>the<br>airway<br>instruments, etc. | Anesthesiologist                                            |                              |

| and<br>other<br>special<br>instruments<br>or<br>equipment. |                        |                 |
|------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------|-----------------|
| 8.<br>Performs<br>surgical<br>hand<br>washing,             | Surgeon                |                 |
| proper gowning and gloving.                                | Scrub Nurse            |                 |

| record the number prior to operation                       |                        |                 |

| of Surgical Safety Checklist.                              | Nurse/Anesthesiologist | Checklist       |

Operating Room (OR)

#### **17. Procedure for Patient Care in the Post-Anesthesia Care Unit (PACU)**

|     | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document                 |
|-----|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|---------------------------------------------|
| 1.  | Receives patient from the operating<br>room:<br>hand-off<br>by<br>the<br>anesthesiologist                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | PACU Nurse                       | Patient ID Wrist<br>Band<br>Patient's Chart |
| 2.  | Monitors and records the following:<br>2.1<br>Initial Vital Signs –<br>heart rate,<br>respiratory<br>rate,<br>oxygen<br>saturation, ECG;<br>2.2<br>Initial Observations;<br>2.3<br>Level of Consciousness;<br>2.4<br>Pain Scale; and<br>2.5<br>Bromage<br>Score<br>(if<br>under<br>regional anesthesia)                                                                                                 | PACU Nurse                       | PACU Record                                 |
| 3.  | Carries out post-operative orders.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | PACU Nurse                       | Patient's Chart                             |
| 4.  | Continuously<br>monitors<br>and<br>documents<br>all<br>observations<br>and<br>nursing interventions.<br>4.1<br>Vital Signs;<br>4.2<br>Level of Consciousness;<br>4.3<br>Pain Scale;<br>4.4<br>Bromage Score (if applicable);<br>4.5<br>All<br>observation<br>and<br>management intervention made                                                                                                        | PACU Nurse                       | PACU Record                                 |
| 5.  | Informs anesthesiologist regarding<br>status and readiness for transfer of<br>patient to ward.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | PACU Nurse                       |                                             |
| 6.  | Evaluates the patient if can already<br>be transferred to the ward (using<br>Modified Aldrete Scoring System or<br>Post Anesthesia Discharge Scoring<br>System)<br>6.1<br>If yes, writes doctor's order for<br>transfer of patient.<br>6.2<br>If not, continuously monitors<br>patient, then evaluates again for<br>status. May have the option to<br>transfer to ICU or special care<br>unit if needed | Anesthesiologist                 | Doctor's Order                              |
| 7.  | Carries out Doctor's Order                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | PACU Nurse                       | Doctor's Order                              |
| 8.  | Informs<br>Ward<br>Nurse<br>regarding<br>transfer of patient                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | PACU Nurse                       |                                             |
| 9.  | Facilitates transfer of patient to<br>ward                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | PACU Nurse                       |                                             |
| 10. | Endorses patient and patient record<br>to ward nurse                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | PACU Nurse                       | Patient's Chart,<br>PACU Record             |

#### **21.General Laboratory Procedure for Histopathology Examination**

| Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document   |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Receives the laboratory request.                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Laboratory Staff<br>(LS)/Clerk   | Laboratory<br>request form    |
| 2.<br>Brings the request & specimen to the<br>laboratory.                                                                                                                                                                                        | Client                           | Laboratory<br>request form    |
| 3.<br>Determines if the request is for in or<br>out patient.<br>3.1<br>If outpatient, proceeds to the<br>cashier for payment.<br>3.2<br>If<br>inpatient,<br>receives<br>the<br>specimen with request.                                            | LS/Clerk                         | Laboratory<br>request form    |
| 4.<br>Receives, verifies completeness of<br>data<br>and<br>encodes/logs<br>laboratory<br>request:<br>4.1<br>If complete, proceeds to Step 5.<br>4.2<br>If<br>incomplete,<br>facilitates<br>or<br>coordinates<br>with<br>source<br>of<br>request. | LS/Clerk                         | Laboratory<br>request form    |
| 5.<br>Logs/registers in the Logbook and<br>assigns Biopsy Specimen Number.                                                                                                                                                                       | Medical Technologist<br>(MT)     | Biopsy Specimen<br>Logbook    |
| 6.<br>Describes<br>and<br>cuts<br>specimen<br>organ/tissue into tissue sections for<br>processing.                                                                                                                                               | Pathologist                      | Histopathology<br>worksheet   |
| 7.<br>Processes tissue section based on the<br>histopathology<br>tissue<br>processing<br>procedure & protocol.                                                                                                                                   | MT                               | Histopathology<br>worksheet   |
| 8.<br>Performs microscopic examination<br>on the processed sample (based on<br>protocol).                                                                                                                                                        | Pathologist                      | Histopathology<br>worksheet   |
| 9.<br>Transcribes and encodes findings and<br>description<br>(based<br>on<br>prescribe<br>protocol).                                                                                                                                             | Pathologist                      | Histopathology<br>worksheet   |
| 10.<br>Reviews printed report form and<br>affixes signature                                                                                                                                                                                      | Pathologist                      | Histopathology<br>Result Form |
| 11.<br>Releases Final Report to Client with<br>claim stub (Results are confidential<br>and released in a sealed envelope).                                                                                                                       | LS/Clerk                         | Releasing<br>Logbook          |
| Note: For Frozen Section, releases<br>the result<br>immediately to the OR-Surgeon.                                                                                                                                                               |                                  |                               |

**Note:** Client refers to either patient, caregiver or healthcare worker for this particular procedure.

#### **Chart No. 21: General Laboratory Procedure for Histopathology Examination Start** Yes Receives the laboratory request Brings the request and specimen to the laboratory Determines if the request is for in our out patient Receives the specimen with request No In patient? Receives, verifies completeness of data and encodes/logs laboratory request Yes Complet No e data? Facilitates or coordinates with source of request Logs/registers in the Logbook and assigns Biopsy Specimen Number Describes and cuts specimen organ/tissue into tissue sections for processing Processes tissue section based on protocol Performs microscopic examination on the sample If Outpatient, proceed to the cashier for payment Department of Pathology/ Laboratory Client Department of Pathology/ Laboratory

Releases Final Report to Client with Claim Stub **End**

Transcribes and encodes findings and description

Reviews printed report form and affixes signature

#### **26. Receiving and Sterilization of Used Articles**

This procedure presupposes that the used articles/items have been cleaned by the endusers. Articles in this procedure may refer to both instruments and supplies that needs to be sterilized. The steps may vary depending on the set-up of the hospital and there can be subprocedures on certain steps that needs to be elaborated. Provided, that the standards are still complied with.

|     | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Person/Department<br>Responsible                                | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                          |
|-----|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.  | Delivers used articles to the CSSD<br>(from<br>clinical<br>area<br>and<br>special<br>areas).                                                                                                                                                                                             | Ward Nursing<br>Attendant                                       | Borrowers Log<br>Sheet/Sterilization<br>Logbook                      |
| 2.  | Receives the used articles from the<br>concerned area/s.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | CSSD<br>Counter<br>Clerk/Nursing<br>Attendant                   | Borrowers Log<br>Sheet/Sterilization<br>Logbook                      |
| 3.  | Checks for completeness of items.<br>Indicates<br>missing<br>items<br>on<br>the<br>borrower's<br>slip.<br>Borrower<br>acknowledges missing items/parts,<br>if any.                                                                                                                       | CSSD<br>Counter<br>Clerk/Nursing<br>Attendant                   | Borrowers Log<br>Sheet/Sterilization<br>Logbook                      |
| 4.  | Forwards articles to the designated<br>washers.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | CSSD<br>Counter<br>Clerk/Nursing<br>Attendant/Utility<br>Worker |                                                                      |
| 5.  | Sanitize hands and wear proper<br>PPE<br>intended<br>for<br>disinfection<br>before<br>starting the procedure                                                                                                                                                                             | CSSD<br>Staff                                                   | Guidelines                                                           |
| 6.  | Washes,<br>disinfects,<br>dries,<br>and<br>inspects<br>articles                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Nurse Attendant                                                 | Guidelines,<br>Issuance slip                                         |
| 7.  | Packs articles/items.<br>Put labels<br>indicating the contents and the date<br>of sterilization according to the<br>manufacturer's<br>instructions.<br>Ensures<br>presence<br>of<br>indicator/autoclave<br>tape<br>to<br>determine<br>if<br>article/items<br>were<br>already sterilized. | CSSD/Nurse/Nursing<br>Attendant                                 | Autoclave Tape,<br>Chemical<br>indicator strip,<br>Sterilization tag |
| 8.  | Categorizes<br>articles/items/supplies<br>into Non-critical, semi-critical, and<br>Critical items prior to sterilization or<br>autoclaving.                                                                                                                                              | CSSD/Nurse/Nursing<br>Attendant                                 |                                                                      |
| 9.  | Places articles in the autoclave/EO<br>Gas/Plasma<br>Sterilizer<br>for<br>sterilization;<br>and<br>follows<br>manufacturer's instruction.                                                                                                                                                | CSSD/Nurse/Nursing<br>Attendant                                 | Autoclave Process<br>Log sheet                                       |
| 10. | Sorts<br>sterilized<br>packed<br>articles/items<br>for<br>storage<br>or for<br>withdrawal/release.                                                                                                                                                                                       | CSSD/Nurse/Nursing<br>Attendant                                 | Guidelines,<br>Biological<br>Indicator Log                           |

| Note: For articles stored, follow the rule<br>"first<br>in<br>first<br>out"<br>based<br>on<br>date<br>of<br>sterilization. The storage<br>must observe<br>aseptic techniques and infection control<br>measures.         |                                                                 | sheet, Surveillance<br>form     |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------|
| 11.<br>Informs units/end-users concerned<br>that sterilized articles are ready for<br>use/withdrawal/distribution.                                                                                                      | CSSD/Nurse/Nursing<br>Attendant                                 | Borrowers Log<br>Sheet          |
| 12.<br>Releases/Dispenses<br>all<br>sterilized<br>articles to respective special areas<br>and wards.<br>12.1Ensures<br>that<br>articles<br>are<br>protected<br>from<br>damage<br>and<br>contamination during transport. | CSSD<br>Staff                                                   | Sterilization<br>Logbook        |
| 13.<br>Records/documents<br>use/withdrawal/release<br>of<br>articles/items.                                                                                                                                             | CSSD<br>Counter<br>Clerk/Nursing<br>Attendant/Utility<br>Worker | Borrowers Log<br>Sheet; logbook |
