### **Chapter 2 Allied Health Professional Service Procedures**

Allied Health Professional Service is composed of professional departments that aim to prevent, diagnose and treat a range of conditions and illnesses and often work within a multidisciplinary health team to provide the best patient outcome. This chapter covers the major procedures under the various allied health departments.

#### **N. Medical Social Work Department (MSWD) Procedures**

#### **30. Availment of Medical Social Work Department (MSWD) Services in the Out-Patient Department**

|    | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Person/Department<br>Responsible                      | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                                             |
|----|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1. | Directly seeks MSWD for assistance                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Patient / Patient Relative                            | Referral Form /<br>Bill Charges                                                                                         |

| 3. | Receives referral from OPD Nurse /<br>attending Physician / Billing                                                                                                                                                                | Medical Social Worker<br>(MSW)                        | Referral Form                                                                                                           |
| 4. | Verifies if patient's treatment is covered<br>by Phil Health<br>and determines through<br>Point<br>of<br>Service<br>Onsite<br>Rapid<br>Enrollment Portal, if membership is<br>active.                                              | MSW                                                   | POS Portal                                                                                                              |

| 9. | Provides<br>appropriate MSW intervention<br>based on Patient's need / problem:<br><br>Enrolls<br>to Point of Service (POS)<br><br>Refers<br>to Malasakit Center<br><br>Psychosocial intervention<br><br>Pre-Admission Planning | MSW                                                   | Form<br>POS Portal,<br>Unified Intake<br>sheet, Referral<br>Form, Progress<br>Report, Daily<br>Accomplishment<br>Report |

#### **35. Procedure on Unit Dose Dispensing**

| Description                                                                                                        | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document       |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Reviews patient's chart.                                                                                     | Pharmacist                       | Patient Health<br>Record          |
| 2.<br>Prepares/updates Patient Medication<br>Profile (PMP).                                                        | Pharmacist                       | PMP                               |
| 3.<br>Checks and validates each drawer of<br>Unit Dose Cart.                                                       | Pharmacist                       |                                   |
| 4.<br>Prepares<br>drugs<br>and<br>medicines<br>sufficient for twenty-four (24) hours<br>dosage regimen of patient. | Pharmacist                       |                                   |
| 5.<br>Prepares Charge Slip.                                                                                        | Pharmacist                       | Charge Slip                       |
| 6.<br>Delivers medicines to ward.                                                                                  | Pharmacist                       |                                   |
| 7.<br>Receives drugs and medicines by<br>requesting ward and affixes signature<br>on the Charge Slip.              | Nurse on duty                    | Pharmacy Charge<br>Slip           |
| 8.<br>Records issued medicines on<br>patient<br>medication profile.                                                | Pharmacist                       | Patient<br>Medication<br>Profiles |

### **Chapter 3 Hospital Finance Service (HFS) Procedures**

Financial management in a hospital setting is the process of seeking the optimal financing, allocation, and control of all resources of the health care organization. The Financial Management Cluster is responsible for financial transactions of the hospital such as: accounting, budgeting, billing and claims, and cash management.

#### **49. Issuance of Statement of Accounts**

| Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Orders patient's discharge and fills up<br>necessary documents.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Physician                        | PhilHealth<br>documents (i.e<br>CF2, CF4)                                                  |
| 2.<br>Forwards Notice of Discharge with<br>necessary documents to Billing and<br>Claims Department (BCD).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Nurse                            | Notice of<br>Discharge,<br>PhilHealth<br>documents (i.e<br>CF2, CF4)                       |
| 3.<br>Receives Notice of Discharge<br>and<br>informs all revenue/cost centers of all<br>scheduled discharges.<br>Note: The term "revenue centers" and "cost<br>centers" may be used interchangeably since<br>this<br>manual<br>is<br>intended<br>for<br>government<br>hospitals<br>that<br>is<br>not<br>necessarily<br>income<br>generating. | Billing Staff                    | Notice of<br>Discharge, PF<br>Charge Slip and<br>PhilHealth<br>documents (i.e<br>CF2, CF4) |
| 4.<br>Forwards<br>remaining<br>charges<br>and<br>clearance slips.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Revenue/Cost centers             | Charge slips and<br>clearance slips.                                                       |
| 5.<br>Collates all charges pertaining to the<br>patient into a Statement of Account<br>(SOA).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Billing Staff                    | Charge<br>slip                                                                             |
| 6.<br>Processes<br>statement<br>of<br>account<br>accordingly and applies all applicable<br>discounts following order of charging:<br>6.1<br>All mandatory discounts (Senior<br>Citizen<br>or<br>PWD,<br>etc.)<br>if<br>applicable.                                                                                                           | Billing Staff                    | Notice of<br>Discharge, PF<br>Charge Slip and<br>PhilHealth<br>documents (i.e<br>CF2, CF4) |

| 6.2<br>Appropriate<br>PhilHealth<br>benefit<br>based<br>on<br>ICD<br>10/RVS<br>code<br>indicated<br>by<br>the<br>attending<br>physician.<br>6.3<br>Other insurance benefits.<br>6.4<br>Medical Assistance.                                                                                                                    |               |                              |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------|------------------------------|
| 7.<br>Prints and issues Statement of Account<br>(SOA).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Billing Staff | SOA                          |
| 8.<br>Explains to patient/caregiver the SOA.<br>8.1Refers patient to the Credit<br>&<br>Collection Unit/MSWD for any issues<br>on excess hospital bill.<br>Note:<br>Refer to<br>the Hospital Finance Service<br>Manual,<br>Chapter<br>11,<br>Billing<br>and<br>Claims<br>Department for the Credit and Collection<br>Process. | Billing Staff | SOA                          |
| 9.<br>Advises patient/caregiver to proceed to<br>Cash<br>Operations<br>Department<br>for<br>payment and clearance.                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Billing Staff | SOA                          |
| 10.<br>Documents data on the summary of<br>bills rendered report.<br>Refer to Chart<br>no. 52<br>for preparation of the said<br>report.                                                                                                                                                                                       | Billing Staff | Summary of Bills<br>Rendered |

#### **54. Processing of Collections and Deposits**

|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------|

| 2.<br>Receives<br>cash/check<br>from<br>clients/creditors/BCD.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Collecting Officer               | Check                                         |
| 3.<br>Issues<br>official<br>receipts<br>(OR)<br>for<br>payment from clients/creditors.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Collecting Officer               | OR                                            |
| 4.<br>Encodes all ORs in the Cash Receipts<br>Record (CRR).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Collecting Officer               | OR, CRR                                       |
| 5.<br>Tallies Cash Collections for the day<br>against Cash Receipts Record (CRR).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Collecting Officer               | CRR                                           |
| 6.<br>Prepares deposit slip/remittance advice<br>for deposit to Authorized Government<br>Depository Bank (AGDB) based on the<br>remittance of collecting officer.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Head Collection Unit             | Deposit Slips                                 |
| 7.<br>Reviews & signs the Deposit Slips<br>(DS).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Head of the Cash<br>Operations   | Deposit Slips                                 |
| 8.<br>For Pick up by Authorized Gov't.<br>Depository Bank (AGDB).<br>8.1<br>If yes, head of the cash operations<br>deposits through pick up by the<br>AGDB the collection together with<br>the deposit slips.<br>8.2<br>If no, requests for transport service<br>from the Engineering and Facilities<br>Management Departments to bring<br>cash/checks to AGDB.<br>8.3<br>For LGU, remits to the Provincial<br>or Municipal Treasurer's Office. | Bonded Collecting<br>Officer     | Deposit Slips                                 |

| 2. | Checks completeness of signatories on<br>the DV and identifies<br>fund source.                                                              | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | DV                          |
| 3. | Prepares payment through checks /<br>Advice to Debit Account (ADA) with<br>Advice of Check Issued and<br>Cancelled<br>(ACIC) if applicable. | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | ADA with ACIC               |
| 4. | Records the checks / ADA to Check<br>and<br>Advices<br>to<br>Debit<br>Account<br>Disbursement<br>Records<br>(CkADADRec).                    | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | Check, ADA                  |
| 5. | Verifies completeness of signature on<br>the DV. Reviews the amount of the<br>check against the DV and SDs. Signs<br>the check.             | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | DV, SDs                     |
| 6. | Forwards the set of documents to the<br>authorized countersigning official                                                                  | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | DV                          |
| 7. | Receives signed Check / ADA from<br>authorized signatories.                                                                                 | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | Check, ADA                  |
| 8. | Secures<br>Official<br>Receipt<br>from<br>the<br>payee and attaches to the disbursement<br>voucher.                                         | Cash of Operations<br>Staff      | Official Receipt,<br>DV     |

Stamps "RECEIVED"<br>and indicate the date of receipt on                                                                                                                 | Accounting Staff<br>(Receiving)  | Purchase Order,<br>OBR/BUR             |
| 2.<br>supplier                                                             | Records in the logbook for PO, with<br>the corresponding number, name of<br>and total contract amount<br>and OBR/BUR number.                                                                                               | Accounting Clerk                 | Purchase Order,<br>OBR/BUR,<br>Logbook |
| 3.                                                                         | Reviews, verifies and checks the<br>propriety of supporting documents.                                                                                                                                                     | Head of Accounting               | Purchase Order,<br>OBR/BUR             |
| 4.<br>OBR/BUR.                                                             | Verifies and checks the source of<br>fund as indicated in the attached                                                                                                                                                     | Accounting Clerk                 | OBR/BUR                                |
| 5.<br>Checks<br>as<br>appropriateness.<br>5.1<br>with<br>5.2<br>If<br>not, | to<br>completeness<br>of<br>supporting documents and as to its<br>If complete, forwards the PO<br>all<br>the<br>supporting<br>documents for processing.<br>returns<br>to<br>originating<br>office with noted deficiencies. | Accounting Clerk                 | Purchase Order,<br>OBR/BUR             |
| 6.<br>contract amount.                                                     | Records in the fund control record<br>book, the PO number and date,<br>name of creditor, and the total                                                                                                                     | Accounting Clerk                 | Purchase Order                         |
| 7.<br>the PO.                                                              | Signs availability of funds portion of                                                                                                                                                                                     | Accounting Clerk                 | Purchase Order                         |
| 8.<br>approval.                                                            | Forwards to Head of Agency for                                                                                                                                                                                             | Accounting Clerk                 | Purchase Order                         |

### **Chart No. 56: Processing of Purchase Order** Forwards the PO with supporting documents for processing Forwards to Head of Agency for approval Complete documents? Returns to originating office with noted deficiencies **Start** Receives and Stamps the PO with the supporting documents Records the PO in the logbook Reviews, verifies and checks the propriety of supporting documents Verifies and checks the source of fund as indicated in the attached OBR/BUR Records the PO in the fund control record book Signs availability of funds portion of the PO Yes No Accounting Department

**End**

#### **57. Processing of Disbursement Voucher (DV) for Payment**

| Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                                                                                         |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Stamps "RECEIVED" and indicates the<br>date of receipt in the face of the DV.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Accounting Staff                 | Disbursement<br>Voucher (DV)                                                                                                                                        |
| 2.<br>Assigns DV number and records in the<br>corresponding receiving Logbook.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Accounting Staff                 | DV, Logbook                                                                                                                                                         |
| 3.<br>Checks<br>as<br>to<br>completeness<br>of<br>supporting documents and as to its<br>appropriateness.<br>3.1 If complete, forwards the DV with<br>all the supporting documents for<br>processing.<br>3.2 If not, returns the DV and supporting<br>documents with<br>noted deficiencies<br>to the concerned office. | Accounting Staff                 | DV, Supporting<br>Documents                                                                                                                                         |
| 4.<br>Indicates source of fund based on the<br>attached<br>Obligation<br>Request<br>(OBR)/Budget<br>Obligation<br>Request<br>(BUR).                                                                                                                                                                                   | Accounting Staff                 | DV, OBR/BUR                                                                                                                                                         |
| 5.<br>Retrieves index if with prior payment.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Accounting Staff                 | DV, supporting<br>documents                                                                                                                                         |
| 6.<br>Checks if with prior payment.<br>6.1<br>If YES, returns DV to concerned<br>office, if ORS/BURS tallies with<br>DV.<br>6.2<br>If NO prepares NORSA/NBURSA                                                                                                                                                        | Accounting Staff                 | DV, ORS/BURS<br>NORSA/NBURS<br>A                                                                                                                                    |
| 7.<br>Reviews<br>the<br>DV<br>and<br>supporting<br>documents, and prepares Journal entries<br>on box B.                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Accounting Staff                 | DV, JEV                                                                                                                                                             |
| 8.<br>Records DV in the index of payment.<br>Initials and forwards to Head of the<br>Accounting.                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Accounting Staff                 | DV                                                                                                                                                                  |
| 9.<br>Retrieves RANCA / RANTA from file<br>and determines availability of Cash.<br>9.1<br>If Yes, reviews and signs box C of<br>DV.<br>9.2<br>If<br>No,<br>retains<br>voucher<br>at<br>the<br>accounting awaiting availability of<br>cash.                                                                            | Head of the<br>Accounting (HOA)  | DV, Registry of<br>Allotments and<br>Notice of Cash<br>Allocation<br>(RANCA) /<br>Registry of<br>Allotment and<br>Notice of<br>Transfer of<br>Allocation<br>(RANTA) |
| 10.<br>Forwards to the Head of the agency for<br>approval.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Accounting Staff                 | DV                                                                                                                                                                  |

| Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                                            |

| 2.<br>Receives and checks the completeness<br>of the documents based on attached<br>checklist and stamps "Received" and<br>indicates the date of receipt in the<br>ORS/BURS. Records in<br>the logbook<br>and forwards to Budget Staff<br>2.1<br>If<br>Yes,<br>verifies<br>availability<br>of<br>allotment/budget<br>based<br>on<br>the<br>Registry<br>of<br>Allotments,<br>Obligations<br>and<br>Disbursements<br>(RAOD).<br>2.2 If No, returns to the concerned<br>office with noted deficiencies. | Receiving/Releasing<br>staff     | ORS/BURS,<br>Purchase Order,<br>Disbursement,<br>Voucher,<br>Payroll,<br>Contract of<br>Service, Logbook               |
| 3.<br>Assigns number on the ORS/BURS<br>based on the control logbook. Records<br>the<br>amount<br>in<br>the<br>Registry<br>of<br>Allotment,<br>Obligation<br>and<br>Disbursement, initials in Box B then<br>forwards all documents to Head of<br>Budget for signature                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Budget Staff                     | ORS/BURS,<br>Logbook                                                                                                   |
| 4.<br>Reviews the ORS and SDs & Certifies<br>availability of allotment and purpose of<br>obligation/ utilization                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Head, Budget<br>Department       | ORS, SDs                                                                                                               |
| 5.<br>Forwards<br>ORS/BURS<br>and<br>SDs<br>to<br>Accounting<br>Department<br>for<br>the<br>processing of claim. Retains copy of<br>ORS/BURS<br>for<br>monitoring<br>of<br>obligation/ utilization status. Refer to<br>Chart No. 55<br>for the Processing of<br>Disbursement.                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Receiving/<br>Releasing Staff    | ORS/BURS, SDs                                                                                                          |

#### **59. Preparation and Submission of Statement of Appropriations, Allotments, Obligations, Balances and Disbursements (SAAOBD)**

| 2.<br>Reviews and Certifies the Report.                                                                                                                                                                                               | Budget Staff                     | SAAOBD Report               |
| 3.<br>Validation/Verification<br>as<br>to<br>correctness of the data entered.<br>3.1<br>If correct, Certifies the Correctness<br>of the report.<br>3.2<br>If incorrect, returns to budget staff<br>for revision.                      | Head of Budget                   | SAAOBD Report               |
| 4.<br>Initials the report and forwards to FMO<br>for approval.                                                                                                                                                                        | Head of Budget                   | SAAOBD Report               |
| 5.<br>Approves the report and forwards to<br>MCC for signature.                                                                                                                                                                       | FMO                              | SAAOBD Report               |
| 6.<br>Approves and signs report. Sends back<br>to budget office.                                                                                                                                                                      | MCC                              | SAAOBD Report               |
| 7.<br>Submits the report to DOH through<br>email on or before the 10th day of the<br>following month.                                                                                                                                 | Budget Staff                     | SAAOBD Report               |

|     | 2.1<br>If<br>with<br>discrepancies,<br>return<br>to |                  |                        |
|     | concerned section for correction.                   |                  |                        |
| 3.  | Based on reports submitted, classifies,             | Accounting Staff | Check & Cash           |

|     | adjustments.                                        |                  |                        |

|     | (JEV). Refer to Chart of Accounts of                |                  |                        |
|     | GAM                                                 |                  |                        |

|     | General Ledgers (GL).                               |                  |                        |

|     | documents to the respective Subsidiary              |                  |                        |

|     | and SLs                                             | (AS)/Head of the |                        |
|     |                                                     | Accounting (HOA) |                        |

### **Chapter 4 Procedures under the Hospital Operations and Patient Support Service (HOPSS)**

The Hospital Operations and Patient Support Service **(**HOPSS) plays an equally important role in the cure and care aspects of health care delivery system through the provision of necessary and timely support services.

#### **A. General Administrative Procedures**

#### **61. Operational Planning**

This process involves all units handling the documents, not just the Chief Administrative Service (CAS). There may be concerns/policies/plans/programs that needs to be presented to the Executive Committee or the Management Committee, while others can be addressed/resolved/approved on the Department/Division Level.

| Description                                 | Person/Department<br>Responsible | Interface/Form/<br>Document |
|---------------------------------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------|
| 1.<br>Notifies concerned staff.             | Chief of the                     | Intra-Office                |
|                                             | Administrative Service           | Memorandum;                 |
|                                             | (CAS) Staff/Planning             | Letters; Hospital           |
|                                             | Officer or Unit                  | Personnel Order;            |
|                                             |                                  | Notice of                   |
|                                             |                                  | Meeting; Email              |
|                                             |                                  | and other forms             |
|                                             |                                  | of acceptable               |
|                                             |                                  | communications              |
| 2.<br>Drafts plans and programs. Submits to | Chief Administrative             | N/A                         |
| Division<br>Head<br>for<br>review<br>and    | Office (CAO)/CAS                 |                             |
| recommendation.                             | Staff, Planning Officer          |                             |
|                                             | or Unit                          |                             |
| 3.<br>Reviews plans and programs            | CAO/Planning Officer             | N/A                         |
| 4.<br>Discusses with concerned staff/units. | Medical Center                   | N/A                         |
|                                             | Chief/Chief of Hospital          |                             |
|                                             | (MCC/COH), CAS                   |                             |

| 5.<br>Presents<br>Operational<br>Plan<br>(OP)<br>to | MCC/COH and          | N/A               |
|-----------------------------------------------------|----------------------|-------------------|
| Executive Committee.                                | Division Heads       |                   |
|                                                     | Concerned, CAS Staff |                   |
| 6.<br>Finalizes plans and programs. Presents        | MCC/COH and          | N/A               |
| consolidated<br>OP<br>to<br>Expanded                | Division Heads       |                   |
| Management Committee.                               | Concerned, CAS Staff |                   |
| 7.<br>Submits to Chief of Hospital/Medical          | MCC/COH and          | Hospital Order or |
| Center<br>Chief<br>of<br>the<br>hospital<br>for     | Division Heads       | Hospital          |
| approval.                                           | Concerned, CAS Staff | Memorandum        |
|                                                     |                      | (draft)           |

| to the appropriate/concerned unit, as               |                      | Outgoing Routing  |

| 4. | Schedules meetings.                                                                     | CAS                                                                                                 | N/A                                                                                       |

#### **64. Decision Making Process**

There may be concerns/requests/queries that need not be submitted to the Office of the Medical Center Chief/Chief of Hospital and can be addressed/resolved/approved on the Division Level (Medical, Nursing, HOPSS and Finance).

| Description                                                           | Person/Department<br>Responsible                                                                    | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Receives request/concerns/queries.                              | Chief of the<br>Administrative Service<br>(CAS) Staff/Chief<br>Administrative Office<br>(CAO) Staff | Incoming and<br>Outgoing Routing<br>Documents Log                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| 2.<br>Assesses problems/issues.                                       | CAS, Division Heads                                                                                 | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| 3.<br>Discusses<br>problem/issues<br>with<br>concerned staff/section. | CAS, Division Heads<br>and concerned<br>staff/section                                               | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| 4.<br>Makes<br>recommendation/s<br>and<br>endorses to the MCC         | CAS, Division Heads<br>and concerned<br>staff/section                                               | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| 5.<br>Approves the recommendation/s or<br>orders other solution.      | Medical Center Chief/<br>Chief of Hospital<br>(MCC/COH)                                             | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| 6.<br>Notifies concerned unit/person.                                 | CAS Staff                                                                                           | Incoming and<br>Outgoing Routing<br>Documents Log<br>(various<br>communications<br>for action and<br>information of<br>concerned<br>areas/Hospital<br>Orders/Hospital<br>Memoranda/Adm<br>inistrative<br>Orders/Administr<br>ative memoranda) |

| 4.<br>The SAO-HRMO reviews<br>and signs the voucher.                                                                                            | SAO-HRMO                                                | st salary<br>1<br>voucher/terminal leave<br>voucher |
| 5.<br>The<br>HRMO<br>Staff<br>for<br>Payroll<br>forwards<br>the<br>signed<br>voucher<br>to<br>the<br>Accounting Section on the<br>set deadline. | HRMO Staff for Payroll;<br>Accounting Section           | st salary<br>1<br>voucher/terminal leave<br>voucher |

| 5.<br>Prepares Trip Ticket.                                                                                                                    | Dispatcher                                                              | Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                                            |
| 6.<br>Forwards<br>to<br>the<br>Chief<br>Administrative Officer (CAO) or<br>Transport Unit Supervisor.                                          | Dispatcher                                                              | Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                                            |
| 7.<br>Evaluates and approves request for<br>use of vehicle and trip ticket.                                                                    | Chief of the<br>Administrative Service<br>(CAS)/Supervisor/Unit<br>Head | Vehicle Request<br>& Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                       |

| 9.<br>Designates the driver concerned and<br>furnishes the driver a copy of the<br>approved trip ticket.                                       | Dispatcher /Supervisor                                                  | Vehicle Request<br>Form; Trim<br>Ticket                                                |
| 10.<br>Checks the vehicle as to readiness<br>and availability of tool kit.                                                                     | Duty Driver                                                             | Daily routine<br>before/after<br>driving; Checklist<br>of Motor Vehicle                |
| 11.<br>Indicates<br>in<br>the<br>trip<br>ticket<br>the<br>beginning mileage.                                                                   | Duty Driver                                                             | Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                                            |
| 12.<br>Furnishes the security guard on duty<br>a copy of the trip ticker.                                                                      | Duty Driver                                                             | Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                                            |
| 13.<br>Checks trip ticket and vehicle before<br>allowing its exit.                                                                             | Security Guard on duty<br>at the gate.                                  | Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                                            |
| 14.<br>Upon return, have the trip ticket<br>signed by passenger; completes data<br>on the trip ticker and reports to<br>motor pool dispatcher. | Duty Driver                                                             | Drivers Trip<br>ticket form                                                            |

**Note:** All trips must be covered by an approved trip ticket prior to the date and time of travel.

#### **E. Property and Supply Management**

#### **90. Procedure on Acquisition by Transfer**

The Property Transfer Report (PTR) is used for the transfer of property from the Central Office to the Regional Office or Hospital. While the Property Acknowledgment Receipt (PAR)/Inventory Custodian Slip (ICS) is used for the transfer of property accountability within the hospital/organization.

| Description                                                                                                                                                            | Person/Department<br>Responsible                                                     | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                       |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Requests transfer of property from<br>other<br>government<br>agency.<br>Writes<br>letter of request to the Head of the<br>benefactor agency.                     | Medical Center<br>Chief/Chief of Hospital<br>(MCC/COH)                               | Letter Request;<br>Deed of<br>Donation/Letter<br>of Intent                                        |
| 2.<br>Checks,<br>inspects<br>and<br>receives<br>property.                                                                                                              | Supply Officer,<br>Inspection Acceptance<br>Committee, Materials<br>Management Staff | Property Transfer<br>Report (PTR)<br>Calibration<br>Report,<br>Equipment<br>Delivery<br>Checklist |
| 3.<br>Signs in the "Received by" portion of<br>the Property Transfer Report (PTR)<br>upon acceptance of the transferred<br>property.                                   | MCC/COH, Supply<br>Officer, Materials<br>Management Staff                            | Property Transfer<br>Report (PTR)                                                                 |
| 4.<br>Forwards the PTR to the Materials<br>Management<br>Section/Property<br>and<br>Supply Section.                                                                    | MCC/COH<br>Materials Management<br>Staff                                             | Property Transfer<br>Report (PTR)                                                                 |
| 5.<br>Requests appraisal of the transferred<br>property if the amount is not indicated<br>in<br>the<br>PTR<br>to<br>the<br>Appraisal<br>Committee.                     | Supply Officer                                                                       | Letter Request<br>and PTR;<br>Appraisal Report                                                    |
| 6.<br>Conducts<br>appraisal<br>and<br>submits<br>report to the Materials Management<br>Section/Property and Supply Section.                                            | Appraisal Committee                                                                  | Appraisal Report                                                                                  |
| 7.<br>Prepares<br>Delivery<br>Report<br>(DR)/Notice of Delivery (NOD) and<br>Inspection and Acceptance Report<br>(IAR).<br>Note:<br>Encodes and print system generated | Supply Officer                                                                       | Delivery Report<br>(DR)/NOD and<br>Inspection And<br>Acceptance<br>Report (IAR)                   |
| IAR, if applicable.<br>8.<br>Requests inspection of the appraised<br>transferred property to the Inspection<br>Committee.                                              | Supply Officer                                                                       | IAR, PTR and/or<br>Appraisal Report                                                               |

| 9.<br>Conducts inspection of the appraised<br>transferred property. Prepares/signs<br>and indicates date of inspection in the<br>"Inspection" column of the IAR.                                                                             | Inspection Committee                                                                     | IAR                                                                                            |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 10.<br>Signs and indicates the date of receipt<br>in<br>the "Acceptance"                                                                                                                                                                     | Supply Officer                                                                           | IAR                                                                                            |
| 11.<br>Submits the IAR with supporting<br>documents to the Commission on<br>Audit<br>(COA)<br>and<br>Accounting<br>Section.                                                                                                                  | Supply Officer                                                                           | IAR, PTR and/or<br>Appraisal Report                                                            |
| 12.<br>Prepares the following:<br>●<br>Stock Card (SC) and Bin Card<br>(BC)<br>for<br>supplies<br>and<br>materials;<br>●<br>Property Card (PC) for Semi<br>Expendable Equipment (SE)<br>and<br>Property,<br>Plant,<br>and<br>Equipment (PPE) | Stock<br>Custodian/Property<br>Custodian/Supply<br>Officer/Materials<br>Management Staff | Stock Card (SC);<br>Inventory Tag;<br>Bin Card (BC);<br>Property Card<br>(PC); Property<br>Tag |
| 13.<br>Submits the IAR, DR, PTR and/or<br>Appraisal<br>Report<br>to<br>Accounting<br>Section. Keeps PTR File of Supply<br>Officer.                                                                                                           | Supply<br>Officer/Materials<br>Management Staff                                          | IAR, DR, PTR<br>and/or Appraisal<br>Report                                                     |
| 14.<br>Records the transferred property in<br>the books of accounts.                                                                                                                                                                         | Chief Accountant                                                                         | Books of<br>Accounts; Supply<br>Ledger Card; and<br>PAR                                        |
| 15.<br>Prepares the following:<br>●<br>Supplies Ledger Card (SLC)<br>for<br>Semi-Expendable<br>Equipment (SE);<br>●<br>Property,<br>Plant<br>and<br>Equipment<br>Ledger<br>Card<br>(PPELC) for Property, Plant<br>and Equipment (PPE)        | Chief<br>Accountant/Accounting<br>Department                                             | Supplies Ledger<br>Card (SLC)<br>Property, Plant<br>and Equipment<br>Ledger Card<br>(PPELC)    |

#### **Chart No. 90: Procedure on Acquisition by Transfer**

![](_page_206_Figure_2.jpeg)

![](_page_207_Figure_1.jpeg)

#### **91. Procedure on Acquisition by Donation**

| Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Person/Department<br>Responsible                                                                                | Interface/Form/<br>Document                                                                                                                            |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Receives Letter of Intent to Donate.                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Medical Center<br>Chief/Chief of Hospital<br>(MCC/COH) or<br>Materials Management<br>SAO                        | Letter of Intent to<br>Donate;<br>Memorandum of<br>Agreement                                                                                           |
| 2.<br>Requests for the following data:<br>●<br>For supplies and materials:<br>name<br>and<br>description,<br>quantity, cost, expiry date, if<br>applicable;<br>●<br>For equipment: name and<br>specification, quantity, cost,<br>status/condition. | MCC/COH or<br>Materials Management<br>Staff                                                                     | Letter Request<br>and List of Items<br>for<br>Donation/Letter<br>of Request of<br>Donation with<br>Specification;<br>Property Transfer<br>Report (PTR) |
| 3.<br>Chooses the needed items from the<br>list.                                                                                                                                                                                                   | End-user/MET, Supply<br>Officer or Engineer                                                                     | List of Items for<br>Donation, Letter<br>Request<br>with<br>Specification                                                                              |
| 4.<br>Prepares Donation Receipt Form.                                                                                                                                                                                                              | MMS Staff                                                                                                       | Donation Receipt<br>Form (DRF)                                                                                                                         |
| 5.<br>Submits<br>recommendation<br>to<br>the<br>Medical<br>Center<br>Chief/Chief<br>of<br>Hospital (MCC/COH).                                                                                                                                      | End-user/MET, Supply<br>Officer or Engineer                                                                     | Donation Receipt<br>Form<br>(DRF);Letter of<br>Recommendation;<br>Letter request;<br>List of Items<br>donated with<br>Quantity and<br>Specification    |
| 6.<br>Approves/Disapproves the Letter of<br>Intent to Donate/DRF based on the<br>recommendation.                                                                                                                                                   | MCC/COH                                                                                                         | Approval Letter;<br>Donation Receipt<br>Form (DRF)                                                                                                     |
| 7.<br>Checks and receives the donated<br>items listed in the Deed of Donation.                                                                                                                                                                     | Supply<br>Officer/Materials<br>Management<br>Staff/Inspector/End<br>User/Inspection and<br>Acceptance Committee | Donation Receipt<br>Form (DRF);<br>Deed of Donation                                                                                                    |
| 8.<br>Requests appraisal of the donated<br>items if the cost is not indicated in<br>the<br>Deed<br>of<br>Donation<br>to<br>the<br>Appraisal Committee.                                                                                             | Supply Officer                                                                                                  | Letter Request<br>and Deed of<br>Donation                                                                                                              |

| 9.<br>Conducts<br>appraisal<br>and<br>submits<br>report to the Materials Management<br>Section.                                                                                                    | Appraisal Committee                                                    | Appraisal Report                                                                |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 10.<br>Prepares<br>Delivery<br>Report<br>(DR)/NOD<br>and<br>Inspection<br>And<br>Acceptance Report (IAR).                                                                                          | Supply Officer                                                         | Delivery Report<br>(DR) and<br>Inspection And<br>Acceptance<br>Report (IAR)     |
| 11.<br>Requests<br>inspection<br>of<br>the<br>appraised-donated<br>items<br>to<br>the<br>Inspection Committee.                                                                                     | Supply Officer                                                         | IAR, Deed of<br>Donation and/or<br>Appraisal Report                             |
| 12.<br>Conducts<br>inspection<br>of<br>the<br>appraised-donated items. Signs and<br>indicates the date of inspection in<br>the "Inspection" column of the IAR.                                     | Inspection Committee                                                   | IAR; Deed of<br>Donation and<br>Sales Invoice                                   |
| 13.<br>Signs and indicates the date of<br>receipt in the "Acceptance" column<br>of the IAR.                                                                                                        | Supply Officer                                                         | IAR                                                                             |
| 14.<br>Submits the IAR with supporting<br>documents to the Commission on<br>Audit<br>(COA)<br>and<br>Accounting<br>Section.                                                                        | Supply Officer                                                         | IAR, DR, Deed of<br>Donation and/or<br>Appraisal Report                         |
| 15.<br>Prepares the following:<br>●<br>Stock Card (SC) and Bin<br>Card (BC) for supplies and<br>materials;<br>●<br>Property<br>Card<br>(PC)<br>for<br>equipment<br>and<br>attaches<br>Property Tag | Stock<br>Custodian/Property<br>Custodian/Materials<br>Management Staff | Stock Card (SC)<br>Bin Card (BC);<br>Property Card<br>(PC); and<br>Property Tag |
| 16.<br>Forwards the Deed of Donation,<br>IAR<br>and<br>supporting<br>documents,<br>Appraisal Report to the Accounting<br>Section.                                                                  | Supply Officer                                                         | IAR, DR, Deed of<br>Donation and/or<br>Appraisal Report                         |
| 17.<br>Records the donated items in the<br>books of accounts.                                                                                                                                      | Chief<br>Accountant/Materials<br>Management SAO                        | Books of<br>Accounts                                                            |
| 18.<br>Prepares the following:<br>●<br>Supplies Ledger Card (SLC)<br>for supplies and materials.                                                                                                   | Chief<br>Accountant/Materials<br>Management SAO                        | Supplies Ledger<br>Card (SLC)                                                   |
| ●<br>Property,<br>Plant<br>and<br>Equipment<br>Ledger<br>Card<br>(PPELC) for equipment.                                                                                                            |                                                                        | Property, Plant<br>and Equipment<br>Ledger Card<br>(PPELC)                      |

| 3. | Prepares<br>stock<br>cards<br>for<br>manufactured supplies.                                                                                                                                                                                     | End-user/Materials<br>Management Staff                            | N/A                                                                                                      |

| 5. | Requests inspection of the items to<br>determine<br>conformity<br>with<br>the<br>report                                                                                                                                                         | Supply Officer/<br>Materials Management<br>Staff                  | Inspection<br>Acceptance<br>Report; ICS/PAR                                                              |

| 8. | Records the fabricated properties in<br>the books of accounts and prepares<br>PPELC.                                                                                                                                                            | Chief Accountant                                                  | Supply Stock<br>Card for ICS and<br>Property Card for<br>Equipment;<br>RPCPPE/RPCI                       |

| 4.<br>Implements the project upon receipt<br>of<br>the required materials.                                                                                                                                                                                       | Engineer                                                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |

| ●<br>List of Scrap<br>and/or unused<br>materials                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                                                               |                                                                                                                |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 6.<br>Requests inspection of the project.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Engineer                                                      | N/A                                                                                                            |

| 8.<br>Submits the Inspection Report with<br>Project Accomplishment Report to<br>Accounting Section.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Engineer                                                      | Inspection Report<br>and Project<br>Accomplishment<br>Report                                                   |
| 9.<br>Submits list and returns unused<br>and/or scrap materials to Materials<br>Management Section/Property and<br>Supply Section.                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Engineer/Material<br>Management Section                       | List of<br>Scrap/Unused<br>Materials/Return<br>Slip for Unused<br>RM/Waste<br>Materials Report<br>for Disposal |
| 10.<br>Acknowledges receipt of materials:<br>●<br>For unused materials, mark<br>the list "Returned to Stock"<br>and record it in the Stock<br>Card (SC) and submits copy<br>of<br>list<br>to<br>Accounting<br>Section.<br>●<br>For scrap materials, prepares<br>Waste<br>Materials<br>Report<br>(WMR)<br>and<br>forwards<br>to<br>Disposal Committee. | Supply<br>Officer/Materials<br>Management Section             | Stock Card (SC)<br>and Waste<br>Materials Report<br>(WMR)                                                      |

| 3.           | Forwards<br>approved<br>RIS<br>to<br>the<br>Materials<br>Management<br>Section/Property and Supply Section.                                                                                                                     | Supply officer/End-user                      | Stock<br>Card/RIS                                                 |
| 4.           | Assigns<br>RIS<br>control<br>number<br>and<br>records in the logbook. RIS number is<br>electronically generated if with HIS.                                                                                                    | Storekeeper/Warehouse<br>man                 | RIS and RIS<br>Logbook                                            |

| 6.           | Issues supplies and records issuance in<br>the Bin Card.                                                                                                                                                                        | Storekeeper/Warehouse<br>man                 | Bin Card                                                          |
| 7.           | Fills out and signs "Issuance" portion<br>of the RIS.                                                                                                                                                                           | Storekeeper                                  | RIS                                                               |

Updates Stock Card.                                                                                                                       | Materials Management<br>Staff                | RIS and Stock<br>Card (SC);<br>Material<br>Inventory System       |
| 10.<br>Note: | Prepares<br>Report<br>of<br>Supplies<br>and<br>Materials issued (RSMI) and attaches<br>copies of RIS and SAI.<br>For those with Hospital Information<br>System (HIS) in place, attachment of RIS and<br>SAI may not applicable. | Storekeeper/Materials<br>Management Section, | Report of<br>Supplies and<br>Materials Issued<br>(RSMI); RIS; SAI |

| 4.<br>Verifies<br>the<br>ownership<br>property through the Property Card<br>(PC).<br>●<br>If<br>the<br>property<br>warranty,<br>supplier<br>notifies the Engineering and<br>Facilities<br>Section.<br>●<br>If the property is out of<br>warranty,<br>documents to Engineering<br>and Facilities Management<br>Section<br>for<br>action. | of<br>the<br>is<br>under<br>contacts<br>the<br>immediately<br>and<br>Management<br>forwards<br>all<br>appropriate                                                                                                                             | Supply Officer/ PAS/<br>ENG Staff          | Property Card<br>(PC); Warranty<br>Certificate                                                                                                                                                   |
| 5.<br>Evaluates<br>the<br>condition<br>property,<br>if<br>repairable.<br>●<br>For in-house repair:<br>a.<br>not,<br>prepares<br>Request (PR);<br>b.<br>upon<br>receipt<br>parts;<br>c.<br>Surrenders<br>appropriate action.                                                                                                             | of<br>the<br>economically<br>Prepares Requisition and<br>Issue Slip (RIS) if parts<br>needed are available; if<br>Purchase<br>Proceeds with the repair<br>of<br>spare<br>the<br>waste<br>materials to the Materials<br>Management Section for | Engineer/Maintenance<br>Staff              | Requisition and<br>Issue Slip (RIS);<br>Pre-Repair and<br>Post-Repair<br>Inspection Report;<br>Equipment Status<br>Report, Purchase<br>Report (PR) for<br>items unavailable<br>or Outside repair |
| ●<br>For outside repair:<br>a.<br>Certifies<br>property<br>defective                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | that<br>the<br>is<br>found<br>and<br>needs<br>outside repair, and that                                                                                                                                                                        |                                            | Certification                                                                                                                                                                                    |

| there<br>is<br>no                           |  |
|---------------------------------------------|--|
| qualified/competent staff                   |  |
| who<br>can<br>perform<br>the                |  |
| repair;                                     |  |
| b.<br>Fills up the Pre-Repair               |  |
| and<br>Post-Repair                          |  |
| Inspection Report;                          |  |
| c.<br>Submits all documents to              |  |
| Property<br>Inspector<br>for                |  |
| appropriate action                          |  |
| d.<br>Prepares and submits PR               |  |
| based in the findings of                    |  |
| the Property Inspector.                     |  |
|                                             |  |
| Note: If the property is not economically   |  |
| repairable, prepares certification that the |  |
| property is beyond economical repair and    |  |

returns to end-user/accountable officer.

#### **100. Procedure in Insuring Government Property**

| Description                                                                                                                                                        | Person/Department<br>Responsible                             | Interface/Form/<br>Document        |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| 1.<br>Prepares<br>the<br>Property<br>Inventory<br>Report<br>(PIR)<br>using<br>the<br>form<br>prescribed by the GSIS.                                               | Supply<br>Officer/Materials<br>Management Staff              | Property Inventory<br>Report (PIR) |
| 2.<br>Approves the report.                                                                                                                                         | Medical Center<br>Chief/Chief of<br>Hospital (MCC/COH)       | PIR Form (COA<br>Form)             |
| 3.<br>Submits report to the GSIS.                                                                                                                                  | Accounting<br>Section/Materials<br>Management Staff<br>(MMS) | PIR                                |
| 4.<br>Prepares<br>Disbursement<br>Voucher<br>(DV)<br>upon<br>receipt<br>of<br>bill<br>of<br>payment of insurance premium and<br>submits to the Accounting Section. | Supply Officer                                               | Disbursement<br>Voucher (DV)       |
| 5.<br>Processes the DV.                                                                                                                                            | Accountant                                                   | DV                                 |
| 6.<br>Prepares and signs the check.                                                                                                                                | Cashier                                                      | Check                              |
| 7.<br>Approves the DV and signs the<br>check.                                                                                                                      | MCC/COH                                                      | DV; Check                          |
| 8.<br>Remits payment to GSIS (Insurance<br>Policy)                                                                                                                 | Cashier / Liaison<br>Officer/MMS                             | Check; Official<br>Receipt         |
| 9.<br>Receives insurance policy.                                                                                                                                   | Accounting/Liaison<br>Officer                                | Insurance Policy                   |
| 10.<br>Submits the insurance policy to the<br>Materials Management Section.                                                                                        | Liaison Officer                                              | Insurance Policy                   |
| 11.<br>Receives the insurance policy for<br>safekeeping.                                                                                                           | Accounting/Supply<br>Officer/MMS                             | Insurance Policy                   |

#### **Chart No. 100: Procedure in Insuring Government Property**
